grazie alla blockchain.</span></span></li></ul><p><span><span>Rispetto ad altre criptovalute LKSCOIN consente di:</span></span></p><ul><li><span><span>Ridurre al minimo le commissioni di transazione legate all\'uso delle principali criptovalute (tendenti all\'1%) che oggi rendono impossibile effettuare micropagamenti nell\'ordine dei centesimi di EUR;</span></span></li><li><span>Eliminare class="icon--not-pressed" focusable="false">\n<use xlink:href="#plyr-play"></use>\n</svg>\n<span class="label--pressed plyr__sr-only">Pause</span>\n<span class="label--not-pressed Foundation is an italian non-profit foundation which goal is to spread the culture of blockchain and promote initiatives that use the principle of sharing information using blockchain technologies and spreading the culture of fintech to innovate sectors such as crowdfunding, ICOs and decentralised finance technologies.</span></p><p><span>To pursue these objectives, LKSCOIN was created, a cryptocurrency structured to have a significant impact on the Internet as it offers the possibility to track and remunerate, through payments and donations, content creators within social networks.</span></p>\n<!-- --><!-- --><!-- --><!-- --></ctv-card-txt><ctv-card-txt card_id="-1" class="ctv-card"><!-- -->\n<p><span>Compared to fiat currencies (EUR, USD, GBP, etc.) LKSCOIN allows you to:</span></p><ul><li><span><span>Bypassing all the problems related to obtaining the various licenses, such as the one called e-money necessary to host a deposit account for third parties within its platform;</span></span></li><li><span><span>Reduce transaction fees related to the use of cards and other suppliers (Paypal, Stripe, etc.) which make microtransactions uneconomic, increasing costs even by 100%;</span></span></li><li><span><span>Make timely payments without having to collect them upon reaching a pre-established threshold or period;</span></span></li><li><span><span>Keep transactions public by ensuring transparency and unalterability of data thanks to the blockchain.</span></span></li></ul><p><span><span>Compared to other cryptocurrencies LKSCOIN allows you to:</span></span></p><ul><li><span><span>Minimize the transaction fees linked to the use of the main cryptocurrencies (tending to 1%) which today make it impossible to carry out micro-payments in the order of EUR cents;</span></span></li><li><span>Completely eliminate the costs and risks of creating a private blockchain, as well as all further problems related to the creation of a proprietary token both in tax and legal terms.</span></li></ul>\n<!-- --><!-- --><!-- --><!-- --></ctv-card-txt><ctv-card-img class="ctv-card forced-height" src="https://media.cam.tv/CID021CFF/profile/images/gmq55e6f8211.jpg?t=-2147483648" style="height: 12.288px;" w2h_ratio="52.08333"><!-- -->\n<ctv-img alt="" class="forced-height" loading_placeholder="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVR42mNkYAAAAAYAAjCB0C8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" src="https://media.cam.tv/CID021CFF/profile/images/gmq55e6f8211.jpg?t=-2147483648" src_placeholder="" style="height: 12.288px;" title="" w2h_ratio="52.08333"><!-- --><img alt="" height="1" loading="lazy" src="data:image/png;base64,iVBORw0KGgoAAAANSUhEUgAAAAEAAAABCAQAAAC1HAwCAAAAC0lEQVR42mNkYAAAAAYAAjCB0C8AAAAASUVORK5CYII=" srcset="" title="" width="1"/><!-- --></ctv-img>\n<!-- --><!-- -->\n<!-- --></ctv-card-img><ctv-card-txt card_id="-1" class="ctv-card"><!-- -->\n<p><span>La LKS Foundation es una fundaci\xc3\xb3n italiana sin fines de lucro que tiene como objetivo difundir la cultura blockchain y promover iniciativas que utilicen el principio de compartir informaci\xc3\xb3n mediante tecnolog\xc3\xadas blockchain y difundir la cultura de la fintech para innovar en \xc3\xa1mbitos como el crowdfunding, la ICO y las tecnolog\xc3\xadas de financiaci\xc3\xb3n descentralizada.</span></p><p><span>El LKSCOIN ha sido creado con el fin de perseguir estos objetivos, una criptomoneda ideada para tener un impacto significativo en la web, ofreciendo la posibilidad de realizar seguimientos y recompensar, a trav\xc3\xa9s de pagos y donaciones, a los creadores de contenido en las redes sociales.</span></p>\n<!-- --><!-- --><!-- --><!-- --></ctv-card-txt><ctv-card-txt card_id="-1" class="ctv-card"><!-- -->\n<p><span>Comparado con las monedas fiduciarias (EUR, USD, GBP, etc.), el LKSCOIN permite:\xc2\xa0</span></p><ul><li><span><span>Evitar todos los problemas relacionados con la obtenci\xc3\xb3n de varias licencias, como aquella del dinero electr\xc3\xb3nico necesaria para recaudar dep\xc3\xb3sitos para otros usuarios en la plataforma;</span></span></li><li><span><span>Reducir las comisiones por transacci\xc3\xb3n relacionadas con el uso de tarjetas y otros proveedores (Paypal, Stripe, etc.) que convierten los micropagos en operaciones poco econ\xc3\xb3micas, aumentando los costos hasta en un 100%;</span></span></li><li><span><span>Realizar los pagos a tiempo sin tener que cobrarlos necesariamente cuando se alcance un umbral o un per\xc3\xadodo determinado;</span></span></li><li><span><span>Mantener las transacciones p\xc3\xbablicas asegurando la transparencia e inalterabilidad de los datos gracias a la cadena de bloques.</span></span></li></ul><p><span><span>\xc2\xa0</span></span></p><p><span><span>Comparado con otras criptocurrencias, el LKSCOIN permite:</span></span></p><ul><li><span><span>Minimizar los costos de transacci\xc3\xb3n relacionados con el uso de las principales criptodivisas (que tienden al 1%) que hoy en d\xc3\xada hacen imposible realizar micropagos del orden de los c\xc3\xa9ntimos de euro;</span></span></li><li><span>Eliminar completamente los costos y riesgos de la creaci\xc3\xb3n de una blockchain privada, as\xc3\xad como todos los dem\xc3\xa1s problemas relacionados con la creaci\xc3\xb3n de un token de propiedad, tanto desde el punto de vista fiscal como legal.</span></li></ul>\n<!-- --><!-- --><!-- --><!-- --></ctv-card-txt><ctv-card-contact-form card_id="1584017459662_vxJPa" class="ctv-card" item_key="lksfoundation" terms_link="" text="Lascia qui di
